done on overlapping blocks.\",\n   114→\t})\n   115→\tm.Duration = prometheus.NewHistogram(prometheus.HistogramOpts{\n   116→\t\tName:                            \"prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds\",\n   117→\t\tHelp:                            \"Duration of compaction runs\",\n   118→\t\tBuckets:                         prometheus.ExponentialBuckets(1, 2, 14),\n   119→\t\tNativeHistogramBucketFactor:     1.1,\n   120→\t\tNativeHistogramMaxBucketNumber:  100,\n   121→\t\tNativeHistogramMinResetDuration: 1 * time.Hour,\n   122→\t})\n   123→\tm.ChunkSize = prometheus.NewHistogram(prometheus.HistogramOpts{\n   124→\t\tName:    \"prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_size_bytes\",\n   125→\t\tHelp:    \"Final size of chunks on their first compaction\",\n   126→\t\tBuckets: prometheus.ExponentialBuckets(32, 1.5, 12),\n   127→\t})\n   128→\tm.ChunkSamples = prometheus.NewHistogram(prometheus.HistogramOpts{\n   129→\t\tName:    \"prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_samples\",\n   130→\t\tHelp:    \"Final number of samples on their first compaction\",\n   131→\t\tBuckets: prometheus.ExponentialBuckets(4, 1.5, 12),\n   132→\t})\n   133→\tm.ChunkRange = prometheus.NewHistogram(prometheus.HistogramOpts{\n   134→\t\tName:    \"prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_range_seconds\",\n   135→\t\tHelp:    \"Final time range of chunks on their first compaction\",\n   136→\t\tBuckets: prometheus.ExponentialBuckets(100, 4, 10),\n   137→\t})\n   138→\n   139→\tif r != nil {\n   140→\t\tr.MustRegister(\n   141→\t\t\tm.Ran,\n   142→\t\t\tm.PopulatingBlocks,\n   143→\t\t\tm.OverlappingBlocks,\n   144→\t\t\tm.Duration,\n   145→\t\t\tm.ChunkRange,\n   146→\t\t\tm.ChunkSamples,\n   147→\t\t\tm.ChunkSize,\n   148→\t\t)\n   149→\t}\n   150→\treturn m\n   151→}\n   152→\n   153→type LeveledCompactorOptions struct {\n   154→\t// PE specifies the postings encoder. It is called when compactor is writing out the postings for a label name/value pair during compaction.\n   155→\t// If it is nil then the default encoder is used. At the moment that is the \"raw\" encoder. See index.EncodePostingsRaw for more.\n   156→\tPE index.PostingsEncoder\n   157→\t// MaxBlockChunkSegmentSize is the max block chunk segment size. If it is 0 then the default chunks.DefaultChunkSegmentSize is used.\n   158→\tMaxBlockChunkSegmentSize int64\n   159→\t// MergeFunc is used for merging series together in vertical compaction. By default storage.NewCompactingChunkSeriesMerger(storage.ChainedSeriesMerge) is used.\n   160→\tMergeFunc storage.VerticalChunkSeriesMergeFunc\n   161→\t// EnableOverlappingCompaction enables compaction of overlapping blocks. In Prometheus it is always enabled.\n   162→\t// It is useful for downstream projects like Mimir, Cortex, Thanos where they have a separate component that does compaction.\n   163→\tEnableOverlappingCompaction bool\n   164→}\n   165→\n   166→func NewLeveledCompactorWithChunkSize(ctx context.Context, r prometheus.Registerer, l log.Logger, ranges []int64, pool chunkenc.Pool, maxBlockChunkSegmentSize int64, mergeFunc storage.VerticalChunkSeriesMergeFunc) (*LeveledCompactor, error) {\n   167→\treturn NewLeveledCompactorWithOptions(ctx, r, l, ranges, pool, LeveledCompactorOptions{\n   168→\t\tMaxBlockChunkSegmentSize:    maxBlockChunkSegmentSize,\n   169→\t\tMergeFunc:                   mergeFunc,\n   170→\t\tEnableOverlappingCompaction: true,\n   171→\t})\n   172→}\n   173→\n   174→func NewLeveledCompactor(ctx context.Context, r prometheus.Registerer, l log.Logger, ranges []int64, pool chunkenc.Pool, mergeFunc storage.VerticalChunkSeriesMergeFunc) (*LeveledCompactor, error) {\n   175→\treturn NewLeveledCompactorWithOptions(ctx, r, l, ranges, pool, LeveledCompactorOptions{\n   176→\t\tMergeFunc:                   mergeFunc,\n   177→\t\tEnableOverlappingCompaction: true,\n   178→\t})\n   179→}\n   180→\n   181→func NewLeveledCompactorWithOptions(ctx context.Context, r prometheus.Registerer, l log.Logger, ranges []int64, pool chunkenc.Pool, opts LeveledCompactorOptions) (*LeveledCompactor, error) {\n   182→\tif len(ranges) == 0 {\n   183→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"at least one range must be provided\")\n   184→\t}\n   185→\tif pool == nil {\n   186→\t\tpool = chunkenc.NewPool()\n   187→\t}\n   188→\tif l == nil {\n   189→\t\tl = log.NewNopLogger()\n   190→\t}\n   191→\tmergeFunc := opts.MergeFunc\n   192→\tif mergeFunc == nil {\n   193→\t\tmergeFunc = storage.NewCompactingChunkSeriesMerger(storage.ChainedSeriesMerge)\n   194→\t}\n   195→\tmaxBlockChunkSegmentSize := opts.MaxBlockChunkSegmentSize\n   196→\tif maxBlockChunkSegmentSize == 0 {\n   197→\t\tmaxBlockChunkSegmentSize = chunks.DefaultChunkSegmentSize\n   198→\t}\n   199→\tpe := opts.PE\n   200→\tif pe == nil {\n   201→\t\tpe = index.EncodePostingsRaw\n   202→\t}\n   203→\treturn &LeveledCompactor{\n   204→\t\tranges:                      ranges,\n   205→\t\tchunkPool:                   pool,\n   206→\t\tlogger:                      l,\n   207→\t\tmetrics:                     NewCompactorMetrics(r),\n   208→\t\tctx:                         ctx,\n   209→\t\tmaxBlockChunkSegmentSize:    maxBlockChunkSegmentSize,\n   210→\t\tmergeFunc:                   mergeFunc,\n   211→\t\tpostingsEncoder:             pe,\n   212→\t\tenableOverlappingCompaction: opts.EnableOverlappingCompaction,\n   213→\t}, nil\n   214→}\n   215→\n   216→type dirMeta struct {\n   217→\tdir  string\n   218→\tmeta *BlockMeta\n   219→}\n   220→\n   221→// Plan returns a list of compactable blocks in the provided directory.\n   222→func (c *LeveledCompactor) Plan(dir string) ([]string, error) {\n   223→\tdirs, err := blockDirs(dir)\n   224→\tif err != nil {\n   225→\t\treturn nil, err\n   226→\t}\n   227→\tif len(dirs) < 1 {\n   228→\t\treturn nil, nil\n   229→\t}\n   230→\n   231→\tvar dms []dirMeta\n   232→\tfor _, dir := range dirs {\n   233→\t\tmeta, _, err := readMetaFile(dir)\n   234→\t\tif err != nil {\n   235→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   236→\t\t}\n   237→\t\tdms = append(dms, dirMeta{dir, meta})\n   238→\t}\n   239→\treturn c.plan(dms)\n   240→}\n   241→\n   242→func (c *LeveledCompactor) plan(dms []dirMeta) ([]string, error) {\n   243→\tslices.SortFunc(dms, func(a, b dirMeta) int {\n   244→\t\tswitch {\n   245→\t\tcase a.meta.MinTime < b.meta.MinTime:\n   246→\t\t\treturn -1\n   247→\t\tcase a.meta.MinTime > b.meta.MinTime:\n   248→\t\t\treturn 1\n   249→\t\tdefault:\n   250→\t\t\treturn 0\n   251→\t\t}\n   252→\t})\n   253→\n   254→\tres := c.selectOverlappingDirs(dms)\n   255→\tif len(res) > 0 {\n   256→\t\treturn res, nil\n   257→\t}\n   258→\t// No overlapping blocks, do compaction the usual way.\n   259→\t// We do not include a recently created block with max(minTime), so the block which was just created from WAL.\n   260→\t// This gives users a window of a full block size to piece-wise backup new data without having to care about data overlap.\n   261→\tdms = dms[:len(dms)-1]\n   262→\n   263→\tfor _, dm := range c.selectDirs(dms) {\n   264→\t\tres = append(res, dm.dir)\n   265→\t}\n   266→\tif len(res) > 0 {\n   267→\t\treturn res, nil\n   268→\t}\n   269→\n   270→\t// Compact any blocks with big enough time range that have >5% tombstones.\n   271→\tfor i := len(dms) - 1; i >= 0; i-- {\n   272→\t\tmeta := dms[i].meta\n   273→\t\tif meta.MaxTime-meta.MinTime < c.ranges[len(c.ranges)/2] {\n   274→\t\t\t// If the block is entirely deleted, then we don't care about the block being big enough.\n   275→\t\t\t// TODO: This is assuming single tombstone is for distinct series, which might be no true.\n   276→\t\t\tif meta.Stats.NumTombstones > 0 && meta.Stats.NumTombstones >= meta.Stats.NumSeries {\n   277→\t\t\t\treturn []string{dms[i].dir}, nil\n   278→\t\t\t}\n   279→\t\t\tbreak\n   280→\t\t}\n   281→\t\tif float64(meta.Stats.NumTombstones)/float64(meta.Stats.NumSeries+1) > 0.05 {\n   282→\t\t\treturn []string{dms[i].dir}, nil\n   283→\t\t}\n   284→\t}\n   285→\n   286→\treturn nil, nil\n   287→}\n   288→\n   289→// selectDirs returns the dir metas that should be compacted into a single new block.\n   290→// If only a single block range is configured, the result is always nil.\n   291→func (c *LeveledCompactor) selectDirs(ds []dirMeta) []dirMeta {\n   292→\tif len(c.ranges) < 2 || len(ds) < 1 {\n   293→\t\treturn nil\n   294→\t}\n   295→\n   296→\thighTime := ds[len(ds)-1].meta.MinTime\n   297→\n   298→\tfor _, iv := range c.ranges[1:] {\n   299→\t\tparts := splitByRange(ds, iv)\n   300→\t\tif len(parts) == 0 {\n   301→\t\t\tcontinue\n   302→\t\t}\n   303→\n   304→\tOuter:\n   305→\t\tfor _, p := range parts {\n   306→\t\t\t// Do not select the range if it has a block whose compaction failed.\n   307→\t\t\tfor _, dm := range p {\n   308→\t\t\t\tif dm.meta.Compaction.Failed {\n   309→\t\t\t\t\tcontinue Outer\n   310→\t\t\t\t}\n   311→\t\t\t}\n   312→\n   313→\t\t\tmint := p[0].meta.MinTime\n   314→\t\t\tmaxt := p[len(p)-1].meta.MaxTime\n   315→\t\t\t// Pick the range of blocks if it spans the full range (potentially with gaps)\n   316→\t\t\t// or is before the most recent block.\n   317→\t\t\t// This ensures we don't compact blocks prematurely when another one of the same\n   318→\t\t\t// size still fits in the range.\n   319→\t\t\tif (maxt-mint == iv || maxt <= highTime) && len(p) > 1 {\n   320→\t\t\t\treturn p\n   321→\t\t\t}\n   322→\t\t}\n   323→\t}\n   324→\n   325→\treturn nil\n   326→}\n   327→\n   328→// selectOverlappingDirs returns all dirs with overlapping time ranges.\n   329→// It expects sorted input by mint and returns the overlapping dirs in the same order as received.\n   330→func (c *LeveledCompactor) selectOverlappingDirs(ds []dirMeta) []string {\n   331→\tif !c.enableOverlappingCompaction {\n   332→\t\treturn nil\n   333→\t}\n   334→\tif len(ds) < 2 {\n   335→\t\treturn nil\n   336→\t}\n   337→\tvar overlappingDirs []string\n   338→\tglobalMaxt := ds[0].meta.MaxTime\n   339→\tfor i, d := range ds[1:] {\n   340→\t\tif d.meta.MinTime < globalMaxt {\n   341→\t\t\tif len(overlappingDirs) == 0 { // When it is the first overlap, need to add the last one as well.\n   342→\t\t\t\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, ds[i].dir)\n   343→\t\t\t}\n   344→\t\t\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, d.dir)\n   345→\t\t} else if len(overlappingDirs) > 0 {\n   346→\t\t\tbreak\n   347→\t\t}\n   348→\t\tif d.meta.MaxTime > globalMaxt {\n   349→\t\t\tglobalMaxt = d.meta.MaxTime\n   350→\t\t}\n   351→\t}\n   352→\treturn overlappingDirs\n   353→}\n   354→\n   355→// splitByRange splits the directories by the time range. The range sequence starts at 0.\n   356→//\n   357→// For example, if we have blocks [0-10, 10-20, 50-60, 90-100] and the split range tr is 30\n   358→// it returns [0-10, 10-20], [50-60], [90-100].\n   359→func splitByRange(ds []dirMeta, tr int64) [][]dirMeta {\n   360→\tvar splitDirs [][]dirMeta\n   361→\n   362→\tfor i := 0; i < len(ds); {\n   363→\t\tvar (\n   364→\t\t\tgroup []dirMeta\n   365→\t\t\tt0    int64\n   366→\t\t\tm     = ds[i].meta\n   367→\t\t)\n   368→\t\t// Compute start of aligned time range of size tr closest to the current block's start.\n   369→\t\tif m.MinTime >= 0 {\n   370→\t\t\tt0 = tr * (m.MinTime / tr)\n   371→\t\t} else {\n   372→\t\t\tt0 = tr * ((m.MinTime - tr + 1) / tr)\n   373→\t\t}\n   374→\t\t// Skip blocks that don't fall into the range. This can happen via mis-alignment or\n   375→\t\t// by being the multiple of the intended range.\n   376→\t\tif m.MaxTime > t0+tr {\n   377→\t\t\ti++\n   378→\t\t\tcontinue\n   379→\t\t}\n   380→\n   381→\t\t// Add all dirs to the current group that are within [t0, t0+tr].\n   382→\t\tfor ; i < len(ds); i++ {\n   383→\t\t\t// Either the block falls into the next range or doesn't fit at all (checked above).\n   384→\t\t\tif ds[i].meta.MaxTime > t0+tr {\n   385→\t\t\t\tbreak\n   386→\t\t\t}\n   387→\t\t\tgroup = append(group, ds[i])\n   388→\t\t}\n   389→\n   390→\t\tif len(group) > 0 {\n   391→\t\t\tsplitDirs = append(splitDirs, group)\n   392→\t\t}\n   393→\t}\n   394→\n   395→\treturn splitDirs\n   396→}\n   397→\n   398→// CompactBlockMetas merges many block metas into one, combining it's source blocks together\n   399→// and adjusting compaction level. Min/Max time of result block meta covers all input blocks.\n   400→func CompactBlockMetas(uid ulid.ULID, blocks ...*BlockMeta) *BlockMeta {\n   401→\tres := &BlockMeta{\n   402→\t\tULID: uid,\n   403→\t}\n   404→\n   405→\tsources := map[ulid.ULID]struct{}{}\n   406→\tmint := blocks[0].MinTime\n   407→\tmaxt := blocks[0].MaxTime\n   408→\n   409→\tfor _, b := range blocks {\n   410→\t\tif b.MinTime < mint {\n   411→\t\t\tmint = b.MinTime\n   412→\t\t}\n   413→\t\tif b.MaxTime > maxt {\n   414→\t\t\tmaxt = b.MaxTime\n   415→\t\t}\n   416→\t\tif b.Compaction.Level > res.Compaction.Level {\n   417→\t\t\tres.Compaction.Level = b.Compaction.Level\n   418→\t\t}\n   419→\t\tfor _, s := range b.Compaction.Sources {\n   420→\t\t\tsources[s] = struct{}{}\n   421→\t\t}\n   422→\t\tres.Compaction.Parents = append(res.Compaction.Parents, BlockDesc{\n   423→\t\t\tULID:    b.ULID,\n   424→\t\t\tMinTime: b.MinTime,\n   425→\t\t\tMaxTime: b.MaxTime,\n   426→\t\t})\n   427→\t}\n   428→\tres.Compaction.Level++\n   429→\n   430→\tfor s := range sources {\n   431→\t\tres.Compaction.Sources = append(res.Compaction.Sources, s)\n   432→\t}\n   433→\tslices.SortFunc(res.Compaction.Sources, func(a, b ulid.ULID) int {\n   434→\t\treturn a.Compare(b)\n   435→\t})\n   436→\n   437→\tres.MinTime = mint\n   438→\tres.MaxTime = maxt\n   439→\treturn res\n   440→}\n   441→\n   442→// Compact creates a new block in the compactor's directory from the blocks in the\n   443→// provided directories.\n   444→func (c *LeveledCompactor) Compact(dest string, dirs []string, open []*Block) (uid ulid.ULID, err error) {\n   445→\treturn c.CompactWithBlockPopulator(dest, dirs, open, DefaultBlockPopulator{})\n   446→}\n   447→\n   448→func (c *LeveledCompactor) CompactWithBlockPopulator(dest string, dirs []string, open []*Block, blockPopulator BlockPopulator) (uid ulid.ULID, err error) {\n   449→\tvar (\n   450→\t\tblocks []BlockReader\n   451→\t\tbs     []*Block\n   452→\t\tmetas  []*BlockMeta\n   453→\t\tuids   []string\n   454→\t)\n   455→\tstart := time.Now()\n   456→\n   457→\tfor _, d := range dirs {\n   458→\t\tmeta, _, err := readMetaFile(d)\n   459→\t\tif err != nil {\n   460→\t\t\treturn uid, err\n   461→\t\t}\n   462→\n   463→\t\tvar b *Block\n   464→\n   465→\t\t// Use already open blocks if we can, to avoid\n   466→\t\t// having the index data in memory twice.\n   467→\t\tfor _, o := range open {\n   468→\t\t\tif meta.ULID == o.Meta().ULID {\n   469→\t\t\t\tb = o\n   470→\t\t\t\tbreak\n   471→\t\t\t}\n   472→\t\t}\n   473→\n   474→\t\tif b == nil {\n   475→\t\t\tvar err error\n   476→\t\t\tb, err = OpenBlock(c.logger, d, c.chunkPool)\n   477→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   478→\t\t\t\treturn uid, err\n   479→\t\t\t}\n   480→\t\t\tdefer b.Close()\n   481→\t\t}\n   482→\n   483→\t\tmetas = append(metas, meta)\n   484→\t\tblocks = append(blocks, b)\n   485→\t\tbs = append(bs, b)\n   486→\t\tuids = append(uids, meta.ULID.String())\n   487→\t}\n   488→\n   489→\tuid = ulid.MustNew(ulid.Now(), rand.Reader)\n   490→\n   491→\tmeta := CompactBlockMetas(uid, metas...)\n   492→\terr = c.write(dest, meta, blockPopulator, blocks...)\n   493→\tif err == nil {\n   494→\t\tif meta.Stats.NumSamples == 0 {\n   495→\t\t\tfor _, b := range bs {\n   496→\t\t\t\tb.meta.Compaction.Deletable = true\n   497→\t\t\t\tn, err := writeMetaFile(c.logger, b.dir, &b.meta)\n   498→\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   499→\t\t\t\t\tlevel.Error(c.logger).Log(\n   500→\t\t\t\t\t\t\"msg\", \"Failed to write 'Deletable' to meta file after compaction\",\n   501→\t\t\t\t\t\t\"ulid\", b.meta.ULID,\n   502→\t\t\t\t\t)\n   503→\t\t\t\t}\n   504→\t\t\t\tb.numBytesMeta = n\n   505→\t\t\t}\n   506→\t\t\tuid = ulid.ULID{}\n   507→\t\t\tlevel.Info(c.logger).Log(\n   508→\t\t\t\t\"msg\", \"compact blocks resulted in empty block\",\n   509→\t\t\t\t\"count\", len(blocks),\n   510→\t\t\t\t\"sources\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", uids),\n   511→\t\t\t\t\"duration\", time.Since(start),\n   512→\t\t\t)\n   513→\t\t} else {\n   514→\t\t\tlevel.Info(c.logger).Log(\n   515→\t\t\t\t\"msg\", \"compact blocks\",\n   516→\t\t\t\t\"count\", len(blocks),\n   517→\t\t\t\t\"mint\", meta.MinTime,\n   518→\t\t\t\t\"maxt\", meta.MaxTime,\n   519→\t\t\t\t\"ulid\", meta.ULID,\n   520→\t\t\t\t\"sources\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", uids),\n   521→\t\t\t\t\"duration\", time.Since(start),\n   522→\t\t\t)\n   523→\t\t}\n   524→\t\treturn uid, nil\n   525→\t}\n   526→\n   527→\terrs := tsdb_errors.NewMulti(err)\n   528→\tif !errors.Is(err, context.Canceled) {\n   529→\t\tfor _, b := range bs {\n   530→\t\t\tif err := b.setCompactionFailed(); err != nil {\n   531→\t\t\t\terrs.Add(fmt.Errorf(\"setting compaction failed for block: %s: %w\", b.Dir(), err))\n   532→\t\t\t}\n   533→\t\t}\n   534→\t}\n   535→\n   536→\treturn uid, errs.Err()\n   537→}\n   538→\n   539→func (c *LeveledCompactor) Write(dest string, b BlockReader, mint, maxt int64, base *BlockMeta) (ulid.ULID, error) {\n   540→\tstart := time.Now()\n   541→\n   542→\tuid := ulid.MustNew(ulid.Now(), rand.Reader)\n   543→\n   544→\tmeta := &BlockMeta{\n   545→\t\tULID:    uid,\n   546→\t\tMinTime: mint,\n   547→\t\tMaxTime: maxt,\n   548→\t}\n   549→\tmeta.Compaction.Level = 1\n   550→\tmeta.Compaction.Sources = []ulid.ULID{uid}\n   551→\n   552→\tif base != nil {\n   553→\t\tmeta.Compaction.Parents = []BlockDesc{\n   554→\t\t\t{ULID: base.ULID, MinTime: base.MinTime, MaxTime: base.MaxTime},\n   555→\t\t}\n   556→\t\tif base.Compaction.FromOutOfOrder() {\n   557→\t\t\tmeta.Compaction.SetOutOfOrder()\n   558→\t\t}\n   559→\t}\n   560→\n   561→\terr := c.write(dest, meta, DefaultBlockPopulator{}, b)\n   562→\tif err != nil {\n   563→\t\treturn uid, err\n   564→\t}\n   565→\n   566→\tif meta.Stats.NumSamples == 0 {\n   567→\t\tlevel.Info(c.logger).Log(\n   568→\t\t\t\"msg\", \"write block resulted in empty block\",\n   569→\t\t\t\"mint\", meta.MinTime,\n   570→\t\t\t\"maxt\", meta.MaxTime,\n   571→\t\t\t\"duration\", time.Since(start),\n   572→\t\t)\n   573→\t\treturn ulid.ULID{}, nil\n   574→\t}\n   575→\n   576→\tlevel.Info(c.logger).Log(\n   577→\t\t\"msg\", \"write block\",\n   578→\t\t\"mint\", meta.MinTime,\n   579→\t\t\"maxt\", meta.MaxTime,\n   580→\t\t\"ulid\", meta.ULID,\n   581→\t\t\"duration\", time.Since(start),\n   582→\t\t\"ooo\", meta.Compaction.FromOutOfOrder(),\n   583→\t)\n   584→\treturn uid, nil\n   585→}\n   586→\n   587→// instrumentedChunkWriter is used for level 1 compactions to record statistics\n   588→// about compacted chunks.\n   589→type instrumentedChunkWriter struct {\n   590→\tChunkWriter\n   591→\n   592→\tsize    prometheus.Histogram\n   593→\tsamples prometheus.Histogram\n   594→\ttrange  prometheus.Histogram\n   595→}\n   596→\n   597→func (w *instrumentedChunkWriter) WriteChunks(chunks ...chunks.Meta) error {\n   598→\tfor _, c := range chunks {\n   599→\t\tw.size.Observe(float64(len(c.Chunk.Bytes())))\n   600→\t\tw.samples.Observe(float64(c.Chunk.NumSamples()))\n   601→\t\tw.trange.Observe(float64(c.MaxTime - c.MinTime))\n   602→\t}\n   603→\treturn w.ChunkWriter.WriteChunks(chunks...)\n   604→}\n   605→\n   606→// write creates a new block that is the union of the provided blocks into dir.\n   607→func (c *LeveledCompactor) write(dest string, meta *BlockMeta, blockPopulator BlockPopulator, blocks ...BlockReader) (err error) {\n   608→\tdir := filepath.Join(dest, meta.ULID.String())\n   609→\ttmp := dir + tmpForCreationBlockDirSuffix\n   610→\tvar closers []io.Closer\n   611→\tdefer func(t time.Time) {\n   612→\t\terr = tsdb_errors.NewMulti(err, tsdb_errors.CloseAll(closers)).Err()\n   613→\n   614→\t\t// RemoveAll returns no error when tmp doesn't exist so it is safe to always run it.\n   615→\t\tif err := os.RemoveAll(tmp); err != nil {\n   616→\t\t\tlevel.Error(c.logger).Log(\"msg\", c.plan(dms)\n}\n\nfunc (c *LeveledCompactor) plan(dms []dirMeta) ([]string, error) {\n\tslices.SortFunc(dms, func(a, b dirMeta) int {\n\t\tswitch {\n\t\tcase a.meta.MinTime < b.meta.MinTime:\n\t\t\treturn -1\n\t\tcase a.meta.MinTime > b.meta.MinTime:\n\t\t\treturn 1\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\treturn 0\n\t\t}\n\t})\n\n\tres := c.selectOverlappingDirs(dms)\n\tif len(res) > 0 {\n\t\treturn res, nil\n\t}\n\t// No overlapping blocks, do compaction the usual way.\n\t// We do not include a recently created block with max(minTime), so the block which was just created from WAL.\n\t// This gives users a window of a full block size to piece-wise backup new data without having to care about data overlap.\n\tdms = dms[:len(dms)-1]\n\n\tfor _, dm := range c.selectDirs(dms) {\n\t\tres = append(res, dm.dir)\n\t}\n\tif len(res) > 0 {\n\t\treturn res, nil\n\t}\n\n\t// Compact any blocks with big enough time range that have >5% tombstones.\n\tfor i := len(dms) - 1; i >= 0; i-- {\n\t\tmeta := dms[i].meta\n\t\tif meta.MaxTime-meta.MinTime < c.ranges[len(c.ranges)/2] {\n\t\t\t// If the block is entirely deleted, then we don't care about the block being big enough.\n\t\t\t// TODO: This is assuming single tombstone is for distinct series, which might be no true.\n\t\t\tif meta.Stats.NumTombstones > 0 && meta.Stats.NumTombstones >= meta.Stats.NumSeries {\n\t\t\t\treturn []string{dms[i].dir}, nil\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t\tif float64(meta.Stats.NumTombstones)/float64(meta.Stats.NumSeries+1) > 0.05 {\n\t\t\treturn []string{dms[i].dir}, nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil, nil\n}\n\n// selectDirs returns the dir metas that should be compacted into a single new block.\n// If only a single block range is configured, the result is always nil.\nfunc (c *LeveledCompactor) selectDirs(ds []dirMeta) []dirMeta {\n\tif len(c.ranges) < 2 || len(ds) < 1 {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\thighTime := ds[len(ds)-1].meta.MinTime\n\n\tfor _, iv := range c.ranges[1:] {\n\t\tparts := splitByRange(ds, iv)\n\t\tif len(parts) == 0 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\tOuter:\n\t\tfor _, p := range parts {\n\t\t\t// Do not select the range if it has a block whose compaction failed.\n\t\t\tfor _, dm := range p {\n\t\t\t\tif dm.meta.Compaction.Failed {\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue Outer\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tmint := p[0].meta.MinTime\n\t\t\tmaxt := p[len(p)-1].meta.MaxTime\n\t\t\t// Pick the range of blocks if it spans the full range (potentially with gaps)\n\t\t\t// or is before the most recent block.\n\t\t\t// This ensures we don't compact blocks prematurely when another one of the same\n\t\t\t// size still fits in the range.\n\t\t\tif (maxt-mint == iv || maxt <= highTime) && len(p) > 1 {\n\t\t\t\treturn p\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// selectOverlappingDirs returns all dirs with overlapping time ranges.\n// It expects sorted input by mint and returns the overlapping dirs in the same order as received.\nfunc (c *LeveledCompactor) selectOverlappingDirs(ds []dirMeta) []string {\n\tif !c.enableOverlappingCompaction {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\tif len(ds) < 2 {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\tvar overlappingDirs []string\n\tglobalMaxt := ds[0].meta.MaxTime\n\tfor i, d := range ds[1:] {\n\t\tif d.meta.MinTime < globalMaxt {\n\t\t\tif len(overlappingDirs) == 0 { // When it is the first overlap, need to add the last one as well.\n\t\t\t\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, ds[i].dir)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, d.dir)\n\t\t} else if len(overlappingDirs) > 0 {\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t\tif d.meta.MaxTime > globalMaxt {\n\t\t\tglobalMaxt = d.meta.MaxTime\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn overlappingDirs\n}\n\n// splitByRange splits the directories by the time range. The range sequence starts at 0.\n//\n// For example, if we have blocks [0-10, 10-20, 50-60, 90-100] and the split range tr is 30\n// it returns [0-10, 10-20], [50-60], [90-100].\nfunc splitByRange(ds []dirMeta, tr int64) [][]dirMeta {\n\tvar splitDirs [][]dirMeta\n\n\tfor i := 0; i < len(ds); {\n\t\tvar (\n\t\t\tgroup []dirMeta\n\t\t\tt0    int64\n\t\t\tm     = ds[i].meta\n\t\t)\n\t\t// Compute start of aligned time range of size tr closest to the current block's start.\n\t\tif m.MinTime >= 0 {\n\t\t\tt0 = tr * (m.MinTime / tr)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tt0 = tr * ((m.MinTime - tr + 1) / tr)\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Skip blocks that don't fall into the range. This can happen via mis-alignment or\n\t\t// by being the multiple of the intended range.\n\t\tif m.MaxTime > t0+tr {\n\t\t\ti++\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Add all dirs to the current group that are within [t0, t0+tr].\n\t\tfor ; i < len(ds); i++ {\n\t\t\t// Either the block falls into the next range or doesn't fit at all (checked above).\n\t\t\tif ds[i].meta.MaxTime > t0+tr {\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tgroup = append(group, ds[i])\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif len(group) > 0 {\n\t\t\tsplitDirs = append(splitDirs, group)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn splitDirs\n}\n\n// CompactBlockMetas merges many block metas into one, combining it's source blocks together\n// and adjusting compaction level. Min/Max time of result block meta covers all input blocks.\nfunc CompactBlockMetas(uid ulid.ULID, blocks ...*BlockMeta) *BlockMeta {\n\tres := &BlockMeta{\n\t\tULID: uid,\n\t}\n\n\tsources := {\n\t\t\tsources[s] = struct{}{}\n\t\t}\n\t\tres.Compaction.Parents = append(res.Compaction.Parents, BlockDesc{\n\t\t\tULID:    b.ULID,\n\t\t\tMinTime: b.MinTime,\n\t\t\tMaxTime: b.MaxTime,\n\t\t})\n\t}\n\tres.Compaction.Level++\n\n\tfor s := range sources {\n\t\tres.Compaction.Sources = append(res.Compaction.Sources, s)\n\t}\n\tslices.SortFunc(res.Compaction.Sources, func(a, b ulid.ULID) int {\n\t\treturn a.Compare(b)\n\t})\n\n\tres.MinTime = mint\n\tres.MaxTime = maxt\n\treturn res\n}\n\n// Compact creates a new block in the compactor's directory from the blocks in 38→\t\"github.com/prometheus/prometheus/model/labels\"\n    39→\t\"github.com/prometheus/prometheus/promql/parser\"\n    40→\t\"github.com/prometheus/prometheus/storage\"\n timeDelta = 30000\n    50→\n    51→type writeBenchmark struct {\n    52→\toutPath     string\n    53→\tsamplesFile string\n    54→\tcleanup     bool\n    55→\tnumMetrics  int\n    56→\n  66→func benchmarkWrite(outPath, samplesFile string, numMetrics, numScrapes int) error {\n    67→\tb := &writeBenchmark{\n    68→\t\toutPath:     outPath,\n    69→\t\tsamplesFile: samplesFile,\n    70→\t\tnumMetrics:  numMetrics,\n    71→\t\tlogger:      log.NewLogfmtLogger(log.NewSyncWriter(os.Stderr)),\n    72→\t}\n    73→\tif b.outPath == \"\" {\n    74→\t\tdir, err := os.MkdirTemp(\"\", \"tsdb_bench\")\n    75→\t\tif err != nil {\n    76→\t\t\treturn err\n    77→\t\t}\n    78→\t\tb.outPath = dir\n    79→\t\tb.cleanup = true\n    80→\t}\n    81→\tif err := os.RemoveAll(b.outPath); err != nil {\n    82→\t\treturn err\n    83→\t}\n    84→\tif err := os.MkdirAll(b.outPath, 0o777); err != nil {\n    85→\t\treturn err\n    86→\t}\n    87→\n    88→\tdir := filepath.Join(b.outPath, \"storage\")\n    89→\n    90→\tl := log.With(b.logger, \"ts\", log.DefaultTimestampUTC, \"caller\", log.DefaultCaller)\n    91→\n    92→\tst, err := tsdb.Open(dir, l, nil, &tsdb.Options{\n    93→\t\tRetentionDuration: int64(15 * 24 * time.Hour / time.Millisecond),\n    94→\t\tMinBlockDuration:  int64(2 * time.Hour / time.Millisecond),\n    95→\t}, tsdb.NewDBStats())\n    96→\tif err != nil {\n    97→\t\treturn err\n    98→\t}\n    99→\tst.DisableCompactions()\n   100→\tb.storage = st\n   101→\n   102→\tvar lbs []labels.Labels\n   103→\n   104→\tif _, err = measureTime(\"readData\", func() error {\n   105→\t\tf, err := os.Open(b.samplesFile)\n   106→\t\tif err != nil {\n   107→\t\t\treturn err\n   108→\t\t}\n   109→\t\tdefer f.Close()\n   110→\n   111→\t\tlbs, err =   120→\tvar total uint64\n   121→\n   122→\tdur, err := measureTime(\"ingestScrapes\", func() error {\n   123→\t\tif err := b.startProfiling(); err != nil {\n   124→\t\t\treturn err\n   125→\t\t}\n   126→\t\ttotal, err = b.ingestScrapes(lbs, numScrapes)\n   127→\t\tif err != nil {\n   128→\t\t\treturn err\n   129→\t\t}\n   130→\t\treturn nil\n   131→\t})\n   132→\tif err != nil {\n   133→\t\treturn err\n   134→\t}\n   135→\n   136→\tfmt.Println(\" > total samples:\", total)\n   137→\tfmt.Println(\" > samples/sec:\", float64(total)/dur.Seconds())\n   138→\n   139→\tif _, err = measureTime(\"stopStorage\", func() error {\n   140→\t\tif err := b.storage.Close(); err != nil {\n   141→\t\t\treturn err\n   142→\t\t}\n   143→\n   144→\t\treturn b.stopProfiling()\n   145→\t}); err != nil {\n   146→\t\treturn err\n   147→\t}\n   148→\n   149→\treturn nil\n   150→}\n   151→\n   152→func (b *writeBenchmark) ingestScrapes(lbls []labels.Labels, scrapeCount int) (uint64, error) {\n   153→\tvar total atomic.Uint64\n   154→\n   155→\tfor i := 0; i < scrapeCount; i += 100 {\n   156→\t\tvar wg sync.WaitGroup\n   157→\t\tlbls := lbls\n   158→\t\tfor len(lbls) > 0 {\n   159→\t\t\tl := 1000\n   160→\t\t\tif len(lbls) < 1000 {\n   161→\t\t\t\tl = len(lbls)\n   162→\t\t\t}\n   163→\t\t\tbatch := lbls[:l]\n   164→\t\t\tlbls = lbls[l:]\n   165→\n   166→\t\t\twg.Add(1)\n   167→\t\t\tgo func() {\n   168→\t\t\t\tdefer wg.Done()\n   169→\n   170→\t\t\t\tn, err := b.ingestScrapesShard(batch, 100, int64(timeDelta*i))\n   171→\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   172→\t\t\t\t\t// exitWithError(err)\n   173→\t\t\t\t\tfmt.Println(\" err\", err)\n   174→\t\t\t\t}\n   175→\t\t\t\ttotal.Add(n)\n   176→\t\t\t}()\n   177→\t\t}\n   178→\t\twg.Wait()\n   179→\t}\n   180→\tfmt.Println(\"ingestion completed\")\n   181→\n   182→\treturn total.Load(), nil\n   183→}\n   184→\n   185→func (b *writeBenchmark) ingestScrapesShard(lbls []labels.Labels, scrapeCount int, baset int64) (uint64, error) {\n   186→\tts := baset\n   187→\n   188→\ttype sample struct {\n   189→\t\tlabels labels.Labels\n   190→\t\tvalue  int64\n   191→\t\tref    *storage.SeriesRef\n   192→\t}\n   193→\n   194→\tscrape := make([]*sample, 0, len(lbls))\n   195→\n   196→\tfor _, m := range lbls {\n   197→\t\tscrape = append(scrape, &sample{\n   198→\t\t\tlabels: m,\n   199→\t\t\tvalue:  123456789,\n   200→\t\t})\n   201→\t}\n   202→\ttotal := uint64(0)\n   203→\n   204→\tfor i := 0; i < scrapeCount; i++ {\n   205→\t\tapp := b.storage.Appender(context.TODO())\n   206→\t\tts += timeDelta\n   207→\n   208→\t\tfor _, s := range scrape {\n   209→\t\t\ts.value += 1000\n   210→\n   211→\t\t\tvar ref storage.SeriesRef\n   212→\t\t\tif s.ref != nil {\n   213→\t\t\t\tref = *s.ref\n   214→\t\t\t}\n   215→\n   216→\t\t\tref, err := app.Append(ref, s.labels, ts, float64(s.value))\n   217→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   218→\t\t\t\tpanic(err)\n   219→\t\t\t}\n   220→\n   221→\t\t\tif s.ref == nil {\n   222→\t\t\t\ts.ref = &ref\n   223→\t\t\t}\n   224→\t\t\ttotal++\n   225→\t\t}\n   226→\t\tif err := app.Commit(); err != nil {\n   227→\t\t\treturn total, err\n   228→\t\t}\n   229→\t}\n   230→\treturn total, nil\n   231→}\n   232→\n   233→func (b *writeBenchmark) startProfiling() error {\n   234→\tvar err error\n   235→\n   236→\t// Start CPU profiling.\n nil {\n   255→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"bench: could not create block profile: %w\", err)\n   256→\t}\n   257→\truntime.SetBlockProfileRate(20)\n   258→\n   259→\tb.mtxprof, err = 300→\tfmt.Printf(\">> start stage=%s\\n\", stage)\n   301→\tstart := time.Now()\n   302→\tif err := f(); err != nil {\n   303→\t\treturn 0, err\n   304→\t}\n   305→\n   306→\tfmt.Printf(\">> completed 311→\tscanner := bufio.NewScanner(r)\n   312→\n   313→\tvar mets []labels.Labels\n   314→\thashes := map[uint64]struct{}{}\n   315→\ti := 0\n   316→\n   317→\tfor scanner.Scan() && i < n {\n   318→\t\tm := make([]labels.Label, 0, 10)\n   319→\n   320→\t\tr := strings.NewReplacer(\"\\\"\", \"\", \"{\", \"\", \"}\", \"\")\n   321→\t\ts := r.Replace(scanner.Text())\n   322→\n   323→\t\tlabelChunks := strings.Split(s, \",\")\n   324→\t\tfor _, labelChunk := range labelChunks {\n   325→\t\t\tsplit := strings.Split(labelChunk, \":\")\n   326→\t\t\tm = append(m, labels.Label{Name: split[0], Value: split[1]})\n   327→\t\t}\n   328→\t\tml := labels.New(m...) // This sorts by name - order of the k/v labels matters, don't assume we'll always receive them already sorted.\n   329→\t\th := ml.Hash()\n   330→\t\tif _, ok := hashes[h]; ok {\n   331→\t\t\tcontinue\n   332→\t\t}\n   333→\t\tmets = append(mets, ml)\n   334→\t\thashes[h] = struct{}{}\n   335→\t\ti++\n   336→\t}\n   337→\treturn mets, nil\n   338→}\n   339→\n   340→func listBlocks(path string, humanReadable bool) error {\n   341→\tdb, err := tsdb.OpenDBReadOnly(path, nil)\n   342→\tif err != nil {\n   343→\t\treturn err\n   344→\t}\n   345→\tdefer func() {\n   346→\t\terr = tsdb_errors.NewMulti(err, db.Close()).Err()\n   347→\t}()\n   348→\tblocks, err := db.Blocks()\n   349→\tif err != nil {\n openBlock(path, blockID string) (*tsdb.DBReadOnly, tsdb.BlockReader, error) {\n   396→\tdb, err := tsdb.OpenDBReadOnly(path, nil)\n   397→\tif err != nil {\n   398→\t\treturn nil, nil, err\n   399→\t}\n   400→\n   401→\tif blockID == \"\" {\n   402→\t\tblockID, err = db.LastBlockID()\n   403→\t\tif err != nil {\n   404→\t\t\treturn nil, nil, err\n   405→\t\t}\n   406→\t}\n   407→\n context.Context, path, blockID string, limit int, runExtended bool, matchers string) error {\n   417→\tvar (\n   418→\t\tselectors []*labels.Matcher\n   419→\t\terr       error\n   420→\t)\n   421→\tif len(matchers) > 0 {\n   422→\t\tselectors, err = parser.ParseMetricSelector(matchers)\n   423→\t\tif err != nil {\n   424→\t\t\treturn err\n   425→\t\t}\n   426→\t}\n   427→\tdb, block, err := openBlock(path, blockID)\n   428→\tif err != nil {\n   429→\t\treturn err\n   430→\t}\n   431→\tdefer func() {\n   432→\t\terr = tsdb_errors.NewMulti(err, db.Close()).Err()\n   433→\t}()\n   434→\n   435→\tmeta := block.Meta()\n   436→\tfmt.Printf(\"Block ID: %s\\n\", meta.ULID)\n   437→\t// Presume 1ms resolution that Prometheus uses.\n   438→\tfmt.Printf(\"Duration: %s\\n\", (time.Duration(meta.MaxTime-meta.MinTime) * 1e6).String())\n   439→\tfmt.Printf(\"Total Series: %d\\n\", meta.Stats.NumSeries)\n   440→\tif len(matchers) > 0 {\n   441→\t\tfmt.Printf(\"Matcher: %s\\n\", matchers)\n   442→\t}\n   443→\tir, err := block.Index()\n   444→\tif err != nil {\n   445→\t\treturn err\n   446→\t}\n   447→\tdefer ir.Close()\n   448→\n   449→\tallLabelNames, err := ir.LabelNames(ctx, selectors...)\n   450→\tif err != nil {\n   451→\t\treturn err\n   452→\t}\n   453→\tfmt.Printf(\"Label names: %d\\n\", len(allLabelNames))\n   454→\n   455→\ttype postingInfo struct {\n   456→\t\tkey    string\n   457→\t\tmetric uint64\n   458→\t}\n   459→\tpostingInfos := []postingInfo{}\n   460→\n   461→\tprintInfo := func(postingInfos []postingInfo) {\n   462→\t\tslices.SortFunc(postingInfos, func(a, b postingInfo) int {\n   463→\t\t\tswitch {\n   464→\t\t\tcase b.metric < a.metric:\n   465→\t\t\t\treturn -1\n   466→\t\t\tcase b.metric > a.metric:\n   467→\t\t\t\treturn 1\n   468→\t\t\tdefault:\n   469→\t\t\t\treturn 0\n   470→\t\t\t}\n   471→\t\t})\n   472→\n   473→\t\tfor i, pc := range postingInfos {\n   474→\t\t\tif i >= limit {\n   475→\t\t\t\tbreak\n   476→\t\t\t}\n   477→\t\t\tfmt.Printf(\"%d %s\\n\", pc.metric, pc.key)\n   478→\t\t}\n   479→\t}\n   480→\n   481→\tlabelsUncovered := map[string]uint64{}\n   482→\tlabelpairsUncovered := map[string]uint64{}\n   483→\tlabelpairsCount := map[string]uint64{}\n   484→\tentries := 0\n   485→\tvar (\n   486→\t\tp    index.Postings\n   487→\t\trefs []storage.SeriesRef\n   488→\t)\n   489→\tif len(matchers) > 0 {\n   490→\t\tp, err = tsdb.PostingsForMatchers(ctx, ir, selectors...)\n   491→\t\tif err != nil {\n   492→\t\t\treturn err\n   493→\t\t}\n   494→\t\t// Expand refs first and cache in memory.\n   495→\t\t// So later we don't have to expand again.\n   496→\t\trefs, err = index.ExpandPostings(p)\n   497→\t\tif err != nil {\n   498→\t\t\treturn err\n   499→\t\t}\n   500→\t\tfmt.Printf(\"Matched series: %d\\n\", len(refs))\n   501→\t\tp = index.NewListPostings(refs)\n   502→\t} else {\n   503→\t\tp, err = ir.Postings(ctx, \"\", \"\") // The special all key.\n   504→\t\tif err != nil {\n   505→\t\t\treturn err\n   506→\t\t}\n   507→\t}\n   508→\n   509→\tchks := []chunks.Meta{}\n   510→\tbuilder := labels.ScratchBuilder{}\n   511→\tfor p.Next() {\n   512→\t\tif err = ir.Series(p.At(), &builder, &chks); err != nil {\n   513→\t\t\treturn err\n   514→\t\t}\n   515→\t\t// Amount of the block time range not covered by this series.\n   516→\t\tuncovered := uint64(meta.MaxTime-meta.MinTime) - uint64(chks[len(chks)-1].MaxTime-chks[0].MinTime)\n   517→\t\tbuilder.Labels().Range(func(lbl labels.Label) {\n   518→\t\t\tkey := lbl.Name + \"=\" + lbl.Value\n   519→\t\t\tlabelsUncovered[lbl.Name] += uncovered\n   520→\t\t\tlabelpairsUncovered[key] += uncovered\n   521→\t\t\tlabelpairsCount[key]++\n   522→\t\t\tentries++\n   523→\t\t})\n   524→\t}\n   525→\tif p.Err() != nil {\n   526→\t\treturn p.Err()\n   527→\t}\n   528→\tfmt.Printf(\"Postings (unique label pairs): %d\\n\", len(labelpairsUncovered))\n   529→\tfmt.Printf(\"Postings entries (total label pairs): %d\\n\", entries)\n   530→\n   531→\tpostingInfos = postingInfos[:0]\n   532→\tfor k, m := range labelpairsUncovered {\n   533→\t\tpostingInfos = append(postingInfos, postingInfo{k, uint64(float64(m) / float64(meta.MaxTime-meta.MinTime))})\n   534→\t}\n   535→\n   536→\tfmt.Printf(\"\\nLabel pairs most involved in churning:\\n\")\n   537→\tprintInfo(postingInfos)\n   538→\n   539→\tpostingInfos = postingInfos[:0]\n   540→\tfor k, m := range labelsUncovered {\n   541→\t\tpostingInfos = append(postingInfos, postingInfo{k, uint64(float64(m) / float64(meta.MaxTime-meta.MinTime))})\n   542→\t}\n   543→\n   544→\tfmt.Printf(\"\\nLabel names most involved in churning:\\n\")\n   545→\tprintInfo(postingInfos)\n   546→\n   547→\tpostingInfos = postingInfos[:0]\n   548→\tfor k, m := range labelpairsCount {\n   549→\t\tpostingInfos = append(postingInfos, postingInfo{k, m})\n   550→\t}\n   551→\n   552→\tfmt.Printf(\"\\nMost common label pairs:\\n\")\n   553→\tprintInfo(postingInfos)\n   554→\n   555→\tpostingInfos = postingInfos[:0]\n   556→\tfor _, n := range allLabelNames {\n   557→\t\tvalues, err := ir.SortedLabelValues(ctx, n, selectors...)\n   558→\t\tif err != nil {\n   559→\t\t\treturn err\n   560→\t\t}\n   561→\t\tvar cumulativeLength uint64\n   562→\t\tfor _, str := range values {\n   563→\t\t\tcumulativeLength += uint64(len(str))\n   564→\t\t}\n   565→\t\tpostingInfos = append(postingInfos, postingInfo{n, cumulativeLength})\n   566→\t}\n   567→\n   568→\tfmt.Printf(\"\\nLabel names with highest cumulative label value length:\\n\")\n   569→\tprintInfo(postingInfos)\n   570→\n   571→\tpostingInfos = postingInfos[:0]\n   572→\tfor _, n := range allLabelNames {\n   573→\t\tlv, err := ir.SortedLabelValues(ctx, n, selectors...)\n   574→\t\tif err != nil {\n   575→\t\t\treturn err\n   576→\t\t}\n   577→\t\tpostingInfos = append(postingInfos, 583→\tlv, err := ir.SortedLabelValues(ctx, \"__name__\", selectors...)\n   584→\tif err != nil {\n   585→\t\treturn err\n   586→\t}\n   587→\tfor _, n := range lv {\n   588→\t\tpostings, err := {\n   606→\t\treturn analyzeCompaction(ctx, block, ir, selectors)\n   607→\t}\n   608→\n   609→\treturn nil\n   610→}\n   611→\n   612→func analyzeCompaction(ctx context.Context, block tsdb.BlockReader, indexr tsdb.IndexReader, matchers []*labels.Matcher) (err error) {\n   613→\tvar postingsr index.Postings\n   614→\tif len(matchers) > 0 {\n   615→\t\tpostingsr, err = tsdb.PostingsForMatchers(ctx, indexr, matchers...)\n   616→\t} else {\n   617→\t\tn, v := index.AllPostingsKey()\n   618→\t\tpostingsr, err = indexr.Postings(ctx, n, v)\n   619→\t}\n   620→\tif err != nil {\n   621→\t\treturn err\n   622→\t}\n   623→\n   624→\tchunkr, err := block.Chunks()\n   625→\tif err != nil {\n   626→\t\treturn err\n   627→\t}\n   628→\tdefer func() {\n   629→\t\terr = 635→\thistogramChunkSamplesCount := make([]int, 0)\n   636→\thistogramChunkSize := make([]int, 0)\n   637→\thistogramChunkBucketsCount := make([]int, 0)\n   638→\tvar builder labels.ScratchBuilder\n   639→\tfor postingsr.Next() {\n   640→\t\tvar chks []chunks.Meta\n   641→\t\tif err := indexr.Series(postingsr.At(), &builder, &chks); err != nil {\n   642→\t\t\treturn err\n   643→\t\t}\n   644→\n   645→\t\tfor _, chk := range chks {\n   646→\t\t\t// Load the actual data of the chunk.\n   647→\t\t\tchk, iterable, err := chunkr.ChunkOrIterable(chk)\n   648→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   649→\t\t\t\treturn err\n   650→\t\t\t}\n   651→\t\t\t// Chunks within blocks should not need to be re-written, so an\n   652→\t\t\t// iterable is not expected to be returned from the chunk reader.\n   653→\t\t\tif iterable != nil {\n   654→\t\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"ChunkOrIterable should not return an iterable when reading a block\")\n   655→\t\t\t}\n   656→\t\t\tswitch chk.Encoding() {\n   657→\t\t\tcase chunkenc.EncXOR:\n   658→\t\t\t\tfloatChunkSamplesCount = append(floatChunkSamplesCount, chk.NumSamples())\n   659→\t\t\t\tfloatChunkSize = append(floatChunkSize, len(chk.Bytes()))\n   660→\t\t\tcase chunkenc.EncFloatHistogram:\n   661→\t\t\t\thistogramChunkSamplesCount = append(histogramChunkSamplesCount, chk.NumSamples())\n   662→\t\t\t\thistogramChunkSize = FloatHistogramChunk\")\n   666→\t\t\t\t}\n   667→\t\t\t\tit := fhchk.Iterator(nil)\n   668→\t\t\t\tbucketCount := 0\n   669→\t\t\t\tfor it.Next() == chunkenc.ValFloatHistogram {\n   670→\t\t\t\t\t_, f := it.AtFloatHistogram(nil)\n   671→\t\t\t\t\tbucketCount += len(f.PositiveBuckets)\n   672→\t\t\t\t\tbucketCount += len(f.NegativeBuckets)\n   673→\t\t\t\t}\n   674→\t\t\t\thistogramChunkBucketsCount = append(histogramChunkBucketsCount, bucketCount)\n   675→\t\t\tcase chunkenc.EncHistogram:\n   676→\t\t\t\thistogramChunkSamplesCount = append(histogramChunkSamplesCount, chk.NumSamples())\n   677→\t\t\t\thistogramChunkSize = append(histogramChunkSize, len(chk.Bytes()))\n   678→\t\t\t\thchk, ok := chk.(*chunkenc.HistogramChunk)\n   679→\t\t\t\tif !ok {\n   680→\t\t\t\t\treturn 685→\t\t\t\t\t_, f := it.AtHistogram(nil)\n   686→\t\t\t\t\tbucketCount += len(f.PositiveBuckets)\n   687→\t\t\t\t\tbucketCount += len(f.NegativeBuckets)\n   688→\t\t\t\t}\n   689→\t\t\t\thistogramChunkBucketsCount = append(histogramChunkBucketsCount, bucketCount)\n   690→\t\t\t}\n   691→\t\t\ttotalChunks++\n   692→\t\t}\n   693→\t}\n   694→\n   695→\tfmt.Printf(\"\\nCompaction analysis:\\n\")\n   696→\tfmt.Println()\n   697→\tdisplayHistogram(\"samples per float chunk\", floatChunkSamplesCount, totalChunks)\n   698→\n   699→\tdisplayHistogram(\"bytes per float chunk\", floatChunkSize, totalChunks)\n   700→\n   701→\tdisplayHistogram(\"samples per histogram chunk\", histogramChunkSamplesCount, totalChunks)\n   702→\n   703→\tdisplayHistogram(\"bytes per histogram chunk\", histogramChunkSize, totalChunks)\n   704→\n   705→\tdisplayHistogram(\"buckets per histogram chunk\", histogramChunkBucketsCount, totalChunks)\n   706→\treturn nil\n   707→}\n   708→\n   709→type SeriesSetFormatter func(series storage.SeriesSet) error\n   710→\n   711→func dumpSamples(ctx context.Context, path string, mint, maxt int64, match 777→\treturn nil\n   778→}\n   779→\n   780→// CondensedString is labels.Labels.String() without spaces after the commas.\n   781→func CondensedString(ls labels.Labels) string {\n   782→\tvar b 797→}\n   798→\n   799→func formatSeriesSetOpenMetrics(ss storage.SeriesSet) error {\n   800→\tfor ss.Next() {\n   801→\t\tseries := ss.At()\n   802→\t\tlbs := series.Labels()\n   803→\t\tmetricName 821→\t\treturn 1\n   822→\t}\n   823→\treturn 0\n   824→}\n   825→\n   826→func backfillOpenMetrics(path, outputDir string, humanReadable, quiet bool, maxBlockDuration time.Duration) int {\n   827→\tinputFile, err := fileutil.OpenMmapFile(path)\n   828→\tif err != nil {\n   829→\t\treturn checkErr(err)\n   830→\t}\n   831→\tdefer inputFile.Close()\n   832→\n   833→\tif err := outputDir, humanReadable, quiet, maxBlockDuration))\n   838→}\n   839→\n   840→func displayHistogram(dataType string, datas []int, total int) {\n   841→\tif len(datas) == 0 {\n   842→\t\tfmt.Printf(\"%s: N/A\\n\\n\", dataType)\n   843→\t\treturn\n   844→\t}\n   845→\tslices.Sort(datas)\n   846→\tstart, end, step := generateBucket(datas[0], datas[len(datas)-1])\n   847→\tsum := 0\n   848→\tbuckets := make([]int, (end-start)/step+1)\n   849→\tmaxCount := 0\n   850→\tfor _, c := range datas {\n   851→\t\tsum += c\n   852→\t\tbuckets[(c-start)/step]++\n   853→\t\tif buckets[(c-start)/step] > maxCount {\n   854→\t\t\tmaxCount = buckets[(c-start)/step]\n   855→\t\t}\n   856→\t}\n   857→\tavg := sum / len(datas)\n   858→\tfmt.Printf(\"%s (min/avg/max): %d/%d/%d\\n\", dataType, datas[0], avg, datas[len(datas)-1])\n   859→\tmaxLeftLen := strconv.Itoa(len(fmt.Sprintf(\"%d\", end)))\n   860→\tmaxRightLen := strconv.Itoa(len(fmt.Sprintf(\"%d\", 864→\t\tfmt.Printf(\"[%\"+maxLeftLen+\"d, %\"+maxRightLen+\"d]: %\"+maxCountLen+\"d %s\\n\", bucket*step+start+1, (bucket+1)*step+start, count, strings.Repeat(\"#\", percentage))\n   865→\t}\n   866→\tfmt.Println()\n   867→}\n   868→\n   869→func generateBucket(min, max int) (start, end, step int) {\n   870→\ts := (max - min) / 10\n   871→\n   872→\tstep = 10\n   873→\tfor step < s && step <= 10000 {\n   874→\t\tstep *= 10\n   875→\t}\n   876→\n   877→\tstart = min - min%step\n   878→\tend = max - max%step + step\n   879→\n   880→\treturn\n   881→}\n   882→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01KBpkEo9TGQ6P3GzuX16fyL","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_016eDHNwbSnS8NTTe99cpPmv","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/documentation.md","content":"# Operational Runbook: Prometheus TSDB Compaction\n\n## 1. Overview\n\n### What is TSDB Compaction?\n\nTSDB compaction is the process of merging overlapping time-series blocks, removing tombstoned (deleted) series, and optimizing the on-disk structure of the Prometheus time-series database. The process is critical for maintaining query performance and disk space efficiency as data ages.\n\n### Why Compaction is Needed\n\n1. **Memory Efficiency**: Head block data is persisted to disk blocks, freeing memory\n2. **Query Performance**: Fewer, larger blocks improve query speed by reducing I/O and index lookups\n3. **Disk Optimization**: Removes tombstoned series and consolidates data\n4. **Space Reclamation**: Unused chunks are dropped during merging\n5. **Overlap Resolution**: Vertical compaction merges blocks with overlapping time ranges\n\n### Compaction Levels and Block Structure\n\nPrometheus uses **leveled compaction** with exponential block ranges:\n\n```\nLevel 0: 2h blocks (HEAD block, freshly persisted)\nLevel 1: 4h blocks (1 compaction, 2 Level-0 blocks merged)\nLevel 2: 16h blocks (2 compactions, 2 Level-1 blocks merged)\nLevel 3: 64h blocks (3 compactions, 2 Level-2 blocks merged)\nLevel 4: 256h blocks (4 compactions, 2 Level-3 blocks merged)\n...and so on\n```\n\nEach block is identified by a ULID (Universally Unique Lexicographically Sortable Identifier) and contains:\n- `meta.json` - metadata (ULID, time range, sample count, compaction level, sources)\n- `index` - label index and postings lists\n- `chunks/` - time-series chunk data\n- `tombstones` - deletion markers for series\n\n### When Compaction is Triggered\n\nCompaction is triggered by three mechanisms:\n\n1. **Time-Based Triggering (Primary)**\n   - Triggered after HEAD block reaches `MinBlockDuration` (default: 2 hours)\n   - Checked on every `Appender.Commit()` call\n   - Set via `db.head.compactable()` condition\n\n2. **Background Compaction Loop**\n   - Runs in a dedicated goroutine (`db.compactLoop()`)\n   - Periodically attempts to compact eligible on-disk blocks\n   - Respects `autoCompact` flag (can be disabled)\n\n3. **Size-Based Triggering**\n   - Triggered if tombstone ratio exceeds 5% of series in large blocks\n   - Triggered if a block is entirely deleted (all series tombstoned)\n\n**Code References:**\n- Triggering: `tsdb/db.go:1120-1126` (dbAppender.Commit)\n- Compaction loop: `tsdb/db.go:1008-1027` (db.compactLoop)\n- Eligibility check: `tsdb/head.go` (head.compactable)\n\n---\n\n## 2. Monitoring Indicators\n\n### Critical Prometheus Metrics\n\nMonitor these metrics on the Prometheus instance itself via `http://prometheus:9090/metrics`:\n\n#### Compaction Success/Failure Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` | Counter | Total compactions executed | Baseline: increases ~every 2h per shard |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total` | Counter | Total compaction triggers | Should grow with `_total` |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` | Counter | Failed compactions | **Alert if > 5 failures/hour** |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_skipped_total` | Counter | Skipped due to `autoCompact=false` | Normal if auto-compaction disabled |\n\n#### Compaction Duration and Performance\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` | Histogram | Time taken for compaction (buckets: 1s, 2s, 4s, ..., 8192s) | Alert if 95th percentile > block range (default 2h) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_size_bytes` | Histogram | Final chunk sizes on first compaction | Min/avg/max should be reasonable |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_samples` | Histogram | Samples per chunk on first compaction | Indicates data density |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_range_seconds` | Histogram | Time range of chunks on first compaction | Should match block duration |\n\n#### Block and Overlap Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total` | Counter | Overlapping block compactions | High values indicate frequent overlaps |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` | Gauge | Set to 1 during block write | Should be 0 most of the time |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` | Gauge | Number of active blocks in memory | Alert if rapidly increasing (unbounded compaction?) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` | Gauge | Total disk size of blocks | Monitor for disk exhaustion |\n\n#### Health Indicators\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_lowest_timestamp` | Gauge | Earliest timestamp in database | Should advance as retention removes old blocks |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes` | Gauge | Max bytes configured for retention | Reference for disk usage |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_seconds` | Gauge | Max retention duration configured | Reference for time-based retention |\n\n### How to Distinguish Healthy vs. Stuck Compaction\n\n**Healthy Compaction Indicators:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` increases every 2-3 hours\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` is well under 2 hours (block range)\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` is stable (not increasing)\n- `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` is stable (typically 10-50 blocks)\n- `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` is stable or decreasing\n\n**Stuck Compaction Indicators:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` stalled (not incrementing for hours)\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` stuck at 1 for > block range duration\n- Prometheus process CPU/memory usage climbing\n- Disk I/O saturated\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` incrementing frequently\n- `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` growing unboundedly\n- Log messages like: \"compaction failed\" or \"aborting block compactions to persist head block\"\n\n### Alert Rules Example\n\n```yaml\ngroups:\n- name: prometheus_compaction\n  rules:\n  # Compaction failures\n  - alert: PrometheusCompactionFailed\n    expr: increase(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total[1h]) > 5\n    for: 5m\n    annotations:\n      summary: \"Prometheus compaction is failing ({{ $value }} failures in last hour)\"\n\n  # Compaction taking too long\n  - alert: PrometheusCompactionStuck\n    expr: histogram_quantile(0.95, rate(prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds_bucket[5m])) > 7200\n    for: 10m\n    annotations:\n      summary: \"Prometheus compaction is taking too long (95th percentile > 2h)\"\n\n  # Blocks not being compacted\n  - alert: PrometheusCompactionNotProgressing\n    expr: increase(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total[4h]) == 0\n    for: 5m\n    annotations:\n      summary: \"Prometheus compactions have not progressed in 4 hours\"\n\n  # Storage growth\n  - alert: PrometheusStorageGrowth\n    expr: rate(prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes[1h]) > 1e9\n    for: 10m\n    annotations:\n      summary: \"Prometheus TSDB storage growing at {{ $value | humanize }}B/hour\"\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Failure Modes\n\n### Failure Mode 1: Disk Space Exhaustion\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Prometheus logs: `no space left on device`\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` stuck at 1\n- Disk utilization at 100%\n- Queries may be slow or fail\n- TSDB cannot persist new blocks\n\n**Likely Causes:**\n- Retention duration or max bytes setting too high\n- Compaction failing silently, blocks not merged\n- WAL (Write-Ahead Log) accumulation without cleanup\n- Monitoring metrics storage exhausting disk\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Check disk usage and available space:\n   ```bash\n   df -h /prometheus-data\n   du -sh /prometheus-data/*\n   du -sh /prometheus-data/wal /prometheus-data/block*\n   ```\n\n2. List blocks and their sizes:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb list -r /prometheus-data\n   # Look for:\n   # - Unusually large blocks\n   # - Blocks outside retention window\n   # - Duplicate time ranges (compaction failed?)\n   ```\n\n3. Check TSDB metrics:\n   ```bash\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep -E \"prometheus_tsdb_(storage_blocks|retention|blocks_loaded)\"\n   ```\n\n4. Inspect Prometheus logs for compaction errors:\n   ```bash\n   tail -f /var/log/prometheus.log | grep -iE \"compaction|disk|space\"\n   ```\n\n**Code References:**\n- Block writing: `tsdb/compact.go:607-718` (write method)\n- Compaction triggering: `tsdb/db.go:1133-1213` (Compact method)\n\n### Failure Mode 2: Compaction Stuck / Not Progressing\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` not incrementing for hours\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` metric stuck at 1\n- Prometheus CPU usage elevated but not responding to queries normally\n- Log messages: \"Head compaction took longer than the block time range\"\n- Compaction duration continuously > block range\n- `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` growing unboundedly\n\n**Likely Causes:**\n- Extremely high cardinality metrics (millions of series)\n- Memory pressure (GC pauses, OOM)\n- I/O contention on disk\n- Corrupted block preventing compaction\n- Context cancellation during shutdown attempting to gracefully stop compaction\n- System resource limits (file descriptors, memory cgroups)\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Check if Prometheus is in compaction:\n   ```bash\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block\n   # Value of 1 means currently compacting\n   ```\n\n2. Monitor compaction duration:\n   ```bash\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds_bucket | tail -5\n   # Check if last bucket shows compactions taking > block_range\n   ```\n\n3. Inspect the HEAD block for compactability:\n   ```bash\n   # Check logs for: \"msg=\"compact head\" duration=X\"\n   # If duration > MinBlockDuration (2h), compaction is slow\n   ```\n\n4. Check system resources:\n   ```bash\n   top -p $(pidof prometheus) # Check CPU, memory, threads\n   lsof -p $(pidof prometheus) | wc -l # Check open file descriptors\n   cat /proc/sys/fs/file-max # System file descriptor limit\n   ```\n\n5. Check for high cardinality:\n   ```bash\n   promtool query instant http://localhost:9090 'count(count by (__name__) ({__name__=~\".+\"}))' 2>/dev/null | tail -3\n   # If > 5 million, this is likely the cause\n   ```\n\n6. Check for corrupted blocks:\n   ```bash\n   # Try to open each block's index\n   for block in /prometheus-data/[0-9a-z]*; do\n     echo \"Checking $block...\"\n     promtool tsdb analyze \"$block\" 2>&1 | grep -i error\n   done\n   ```\n\n**Code References:**\n- Compaction check: `tsdb/db.go:1162-1164` (if !db.head.compactable())\n- Duration warning: `tsdb/db.go:1197-1202` (compaction duration > block range warning)\n- Block population: `tsdb/compact.go:729-875` (PopulateBlock method)\n\n### Failure Mode 3: Block Corruption\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Queries fail with errors about corrupted indices or chunks\n- Compaction fails when trying to compact specific blocks\n- Log messages: `open index reader`, `chunk`, `series` errors\n- `promtool tsdb analyze` shows errors\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` incrementing\n\n**Likely Causes:**\n- Unclean shutdown during block write (power loss, SIGKILL)\n- Corrupted meta.json file\n- Corrupted index or chunks file\n- Incomplete block rename operation\n- filesystem corruption\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Identify which block is corrupted:\n   ```bash\n   # Check all blocks\n   for block in /prometheus-data/[0-9a-z]*; do\n     if ! promtool tsdb analyze \"$block\" > /dev/null 2>&1; then\n       echo \"Corrupted: $block\"\n     fi\n   done\n   ```\n\n2. Inspect meta.json:\n   ```bash\n   cat /prometheus-data/BLOCK_ULID/meta.json | jq .\n   # Check for: ULID, MinTime, MaxTime, Stats, Compaction.Level\n   ```\n\n3. Check if block is marked Deletable:\n   ```bash\n   cat /prometheus-data/BLOCK_ULID/meta.json | jq '.Compaction.Deletable'\n   # true = block is marked for deletion\n   ```\n\n4. Try to read block index directly:\n   ```bash\n   # This will fail if index is corrupted\n   promtool tsdb analyze --limit=1 /prometheus-data/BLOCK_ULID\n   ```\n\n**Code References:**\n- Block opening: `tsdb/block.go` (OpenBlock function)\n- Meta file reading: `tsdb/db.go` (readMetaFile function)\n- Repair function: `tsdb/repair.go:30-124` (repairBadIndexVersion)\n\n### Failure Mode 4: Out-of-Memory (OOM) During Compaction\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Prometheus process killed with signal 9\n- System logs show \"Out of memory: Kill process\"\n- Incomplete blocks left on disk (meta.json.tmp or chunks.tmp)\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` stuck at 1\n- Memory usage spikes during compaction window\n\n**Likely Causes:**\n- Very high cardinality metrics (millions of unique series)\n- Large time range blocks with dense data\n- Insufficient memory allocated to Prometheus\n- Memory leak in compaction path\n- Simultaneous compaction of too many series\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Check Prometheus memory limits:\n   ```bash\n   # From Kubernetes\n   kubectl describe pod PROMETHEUS_POD | grep -A 5 \"memory:\"\n\n   # From systemd\n   systemctl status prometheus | grep Memory\n\n   # From process\n   ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep\n   cat /proc/PID/limits | grep memory\n   ```\n\n2. Check peak memory during compaction:\n   ```bash\n   # Monitor in real-time\n   watch -n 1 'ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep | awk \"{print \\$6}\"'\n   ```\n\n3. Estimate memory needed:\n   ```bash\n   # Count series in largest block\n   for block in /prometheus-data/[0-9a-z]*; do\n     series=$(jq '.Stats.NumSeries' \"$block/meta.json\")\n     echo \"$block: $series series\"\n   done | sort -k2 -nr | head -3\n   # Rough estimate: 1 million series needs 2-4 GB\n   ```\n\n4. Check if out-of-order (OOO) compaction is enabled:\n   ```bash\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep -i \"out.of.order\"\n   # OOO compaction uses additional memory\n   ```\n\n**Code References:**\n- Block population (memory intensive): `tsdb/compact.go:729-875` (PopulateBlock)\n- OOO compaction: `tsdb/db.go:1238-1283` (compactOOOHead)\n- Chunk merging: `tsdb/compact.go:819-823` (NewMergeChunkSeriesSet)\n\n---\n\n## 4. Recovery Procedures\n\n### Recovery for Failure Mode 1: Disk Space Exhaustion\n\n**Recovery Steps:**\n\n1. **Immediate Actions (within minutes)**\n   ```bash\n   # Stop any additional writes\n   sudo systemctl stop prometheus\n   # This prevents new blocks being created\n   ```\n\n2. **Identify and Remove Old Blocks**\n   ```bash\n   # List all blocks with human-readable dates\n   promtool tsdb list -r /prometheus-data | head -20\n\n   # Identify blocks outside retention window\n   # Calculate which blocks to delete:\n   # retention_duration = 15 days (default)\n   # current_timestamp = $(date +%s)000  (milliseconds)\n   # block_max_time < (current_timestamp - retention_duration)\n\n   RETENTION_MS=$((15 * 24 * 3600 * 1000))  # 15 days in ms\n   CURRENT_MS=$(date +%s)000\n   CUTOFF=$((CURRENT_MS - RETENTION_MS))\n\n   # Find blocks to delete\n   for block in /prometheus-data/[0-9a-z]*; do\n     max_time=$(jq '.MaxTime' \"$block/meta.json\")\n     if [ \"$max_time\" -lt \"$CUTOFF\" ]; then\n       echo \"DELETE: $block (max_time=$max_time < $CUTOFF)\"\n     fi\n   done\n   ```\n\n3. **Delete Oldest Blocks**\n   ```bash\n   # BE CAREFUL: Manual deletion of blocks\n   # Always backup first\n   tar czf /backup/prometheus-blocks-$(date +%s).tar.gz /prometheus-data\n\n   # Delete by ULID (from step 2 above)\n   rm -rf /prometheus-data/01ARZ3NDEKTSV4RRFFQ69G5FAV  # Example ULID\n   rm -rf /prometheus-data/*.tmp-for-deletion\n   rm -rf /prometheus-data/*.tmp-for-creation\n   ```\n\n4. **Clean Up WAL and Temporary Files**\n   ```bash\n   # Remove incomplete compaction artifacts\n   find /prometheus-data -name \"*.tmp\" -delete\n   find /prometheus-data -name \"*.tmp-for-*\" -delete\n\n   # WAL cleanup (if safe)\n   # Only if no recovery is needed:\n   rm -rf /prometheus-data/wal/*\n   # WARNING: This loses recent uncompacted data\n   ```\n\n5. **Adjust Configuration**\n   ```yaml\n   # Edit /etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml or Helm values\n   global:\n     external_labels:\n       cluster: 'my-cluster'\n\n   storage:\n     tsdb:\n       retention:\n         time: 7d  # Reduce from 15d to 7d\n         # OR\n         size: '50GB'  # Cap at 50GB instead of unlimited\n   ```\n\n6. **Restart Prometheus**\n   ```bash\n   # Verify disk space\n   df -h /prometheus-data  # Should have space now\n\n   # Restart with new retention\n   sudo systemctl start prometheus\n\n   # Verify startup\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/status/config | jq .\n   ```\n\n7. **Monitor Recovery**\n   ```bash\n   # Watch compaction progress\n   watch -n 5 'curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | \\\n     grep \"prometheus_tsdb_\\(blocks_loaded\\|storage_blocks_bytes\\|compactions_total\\)\"'\n\n   # Should see:\n   # - storage_blocks_bytes decreasing\n   # - blocks_loaded stable\n   # - compactions_total incrementing\n   ```\n\n**Testing Recovery:**\n```bash\n# After 30 minutes, verify:\n1. Disk space stabilized: df -h /prometheus-data\n2. Queries working: curl http://localhost:9090/api/v1/instant_query?query=up\n3. No new errors in logs: tail -f /var/log/prometheus.log\n```\n\n### Recovery for Failure Mode 2: Compaction Stuck / Not Progressing\n\n**Recovery Steps:**\n\n1. **Assess Current State**\n   ```bash\n   # Check if Prometheus is still running\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/-/healthy\n   # 200 OK = responsive, connection refused = down\n\n   # Check if in compaction\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block\n   ```\n\n2. **Option A: Graceful Restart (Preferred)**\n   ```bash\n   # This allows in-flight compaction to finish (with timeout)\n   systemctl stop prometheus  # Default 90s timeout\n\n   # Wait for graceful shutdown (check logs)\n   sleep 120\n\n   # Verify it's down\n   pgrep -f prometheus || echo \"Prometheus stopped\"\n\n   # Check if any compaction artifacts remain\n   ls -la /prometheus-data/*.tmp* 2>/dev/null\n\n   # Clean up incomplete blocks\n   find /prometheus-data -name \"*.tmp-for-creation\" -exec rm -rf {} \\;\n\n   # Start again\n   systemctl start prometheus\n\n   # Watch compaction\n   watch -n 2 'curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total'\n   ```\n\n3. **Option B: Force Kill (If Graceful Fails)**\n   ```bash\n   # Only if graceful stop doesn't work after 5 minutes\n   kill -9 $(pgrep -f prometheus)\n\n   # Wait for process to die\n   sleep 5\n\n   # Check for corrupted blocks\n   for block in /prometheus-data/[0-9a-z]*; do\n     if [ -d \"$block\" ] && [ -f \"$block/meta.json\" ]; then\n       state=$(jq -r '.Compaction.Failed // false' \"$block/meta.json\")\n       if [ \"$state\" = \"true\" ]; then\n         echo \"Mark for deletion (failed): $block\"\n         # Optional: delete failed block\n         # rm -rf \"$block\"\n       fi\n     fi\n   done\n\n   # Clean up temporary files\n   rm -rf /prometheus-data/*.tmp-for-*\n\n   # Restart\n   systemctl start prometheus\n   ```\n\n4. **Monitor for Resolution**\n   ```bash\n   # Watch these metrics improve over time:\n   watch -n 10 'curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep -E \\\n     \"prometheus_tsdb_(compactions_total|compaction_duration|blocks_loaded|compactions_failed)\" | \\\n     grep -v bucket'\n\n   # Expected improvements:\n   # - compactions_total increases every 5-30 min\n   # - compaction_duration decreases\n   # - blocks_loaded stabilizes\n   # - compactions_failed stops incrementing\n   ```\n\n5. **If Compaction Still Stuck After Restart**\n   ```bash\n   # Reduce data to make compaction faster\n   # Option 1: Lower retention\n   storage:\n     tsdb:\n       retention:\n         time: 3d  # Very aggressive\n\n   # Option 2: Scale down high-cardinality scrape jobs\n   # Edit prometheus.yml to comment out expensive targets\n\n   # Restart again\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n   ```\n\n**Prevention:**\n```yaml\n# Add memory limits to Prometheus deployment\nresources:\n  requests:\n    memory: \"16Gi\"   # For high cardinality\n    cpu: \"4\"\n  limits:\n    memory: \"32Gi\"   # Headroom for compaction spikes\n    cpu: \"8\"\n\n# Monitor early:\nstorage:\n  tsdb:\n    wal_compression: snappy  # Reduce WAL size\n    samples_per_chunk: 4096  # Increase density\n```\n\n### Recovery for Failure Mode 3: Block Corruption\n\n**Recovery Steps:**\n\n1. **Identify Corrupted Block**\n   ```bash\n   # Test all blocks\n   corrupted_blocks=()\n   for block in /prometheus-data/[0-9a-z]*; do\n     if ! promtool tsdb analyze --limit=1 \"$block\" > /dev/null 2>&1; then\n       corrupted_blocks+=(\"$block\")\n       echo \"CORRUPTED: $(basename $block)\"\n     fi\n   done\n\n   # If no corrupted blocks found, try to open with database\n   # Restart Prometheus to trigger validation\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n\n   # Check logs for errors\n   grep -i \"error\\|corrupted\" /var/log/prometheus.log | tail -20\n   ```\n\n2. **Isolate Corrupted Block**\n   ```bash\n   # Move corrupted block to quarantine\n   mkdir -p /prometheus-data/quarantine\n\n   for block in \"${corrupted_blocks[@]}\"; do\n     mv \"$block\" /prometheus-data/quarantine/\n     echo \"Quarantined: $(basename $block)\"\n   done\n\n   # Restart Prometheus (it will skip missing blocks)\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n\n   # Verify recovery\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/-/healthy\n   ```\n\n3. **Option A: Delete Corrupted Block (Data Loss)**\n   ```bash\n   # If block is outside retention or duplicated\n   rm -rf /prometheus-data/quarantine/*\n\n   # Restart Prometheus\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n\n   # Compaction will eventually compact remaining blocks\n   ```\n\n4. **Option B: Attempt Repair (Metadata Fix)**\n   ```bash\n   # If only meta.json is corrupted, try to reconstruct\n   block_ulid=\"01ARZ3NDEKTSV4RRFFQ69G5FAV\"  # Example\n\n   # Check if index and chunks exist\n   ls -la /prometheus-data/$block_ulid/index\n   ls -la /prometheus-data/$block_ulid/chunks/\n\n   # Try to rebuild meta.json by opening with read-only DB\n   cd /tmp && python3 << 'EOF'\n   import json\n   import os\n\n   # Read index to estimate stats\n   # This is manual, usually better to just delete\n   print(\"Manual repair needed - block structure unclear\")\n   EOF\n   ```\n\n5. **Option C: Use Promtool to Clean Up**\n   ```bash\n   # Prometheus 2.50+ has better recovery\n   # Run database health check\n   promtool tsdb list /prometheus-data\n\n   # If many blocks are corrupted, consider fresh start\n   # (Only if you have alerting backups!)\n   ```\n\n6. **Restart and Verify**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n\n   # Check metrics availability\n   curl -s 'http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query?query=up' | jq '.data.result | length'\n\n   # Should return non-zero results\n\n   # Monitor compaction to recover\n   watch -n 30 'curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | \\\n     grep \"prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded\\|prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes\"'\n   ```\n\n**Prevention:**\n```bash\n# Enable filesystem integrity checks\n# On Linux with ext4:\ntune2fs -c 20 /dev/mapper/prometheus-data  # Check every 20 mounts\ntune2fs -i 1m /dev/mapper/prometheus-data  # Check every month\n\n# Regular backups\n0 2 * * * tar -czf /backups/prometheus-$(date +\\%Y\\%m\\%d).tar.gz /prometheus-data\n\n# Monitor SMART health (for hard drives)\nsmartctl -H /dev/sda  # Daily monitoring recommended\n```\n\n### Recovery for Failure Mode 4: Out-of-Memory (OOM) During Compaction\n\n**Recovery Steps:**\n\n1. **Immediate Recovery**\n   ```bash\n   # Prometheus was likely killed, restart it\n   # First, check if process is still running\n   pgrep -f prometheus && kill -9 $(pgrep -f prometheus)\n\n   # Wait for graceful shutdown signals to be processed\n   sleep 10\n\n   # Clean up temporary blocks\n   rm -rf /prometheus-data/*.tmp-for-*\n   ```\n\n2. **Increase Memory Allocation**\n   ```bash\n   # For Kubernetes\n   kubectl set resources deployment prometheus \\\n     --limits=memory=64Gi \\\n     --requests=memory=32Gi\n   # Restart pods: kubectl delete pod -l app=prometheus\n\n   # For Docker\n   docker update --memory 64g CONTAINER_ID\n\n   # For systemd\n   # Edit /etc/systemd/system/prometheus.service\n   # Add or modify:\n   [Service]\n   MemoryMax=64G\n   MemoryHigh=48G\n\n   systemctl daemon-reload\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n   ```\n\n3. **Reduce Cardinality Before Restart**\n   ```bash\n   # Identify high-cardinality metrics\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/series?match[]={__name__=~'.+'} 2>/dev/null | \\\n     jq '.data | group_by(.[0]) | map({metric: .[0], count: length}) | \\\n     sort_by(.count) | reverse | .[0:10]'\n\n   # Or use promtool (if DB is readable)\n   promtool tsdb analyze /prometheus-data --limit=10\n   ```\n\n4. **Adjust Configuration to Reduce Memory**\n   ```yaml\n   # Edit /etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml\n   storage:\n     tsdb:\n       retention:\n         time: 3d  # Reduce from 15d\n       max_block_duration: 1h  # More frequent compactions, smaller blocks\n       min_block_duration: 1h   # Smaller blocks = less memory\n\n   # Disable out-of-order samples (if enabled)\n   # out_of_order_time_window: 0  # Saves memory for OOO compaction\n\n   # Reduce scrape frequency for high-cardinality jobs\n   # In scrape_configs:\n   - job_name: 'high-cardinality'\n     scrape_interval: 2m  # Instead of 15s\n     scrape_timeout: 10s\n   ```\n\n5. **Filter High-Cardinality Metrics**\n   ```yaml\n   # Use metric relabeling to drop expensive metrics\n   scrape_configs:\n   - job_name: 'kubernetes-pods'\n     metric_relabel_configs:\n     # Drop high-cardinality label combinations\n     - source_labels: [__name__]\n       regex: 'process_.*_bucket'  # Drop histogram buckets\n       action: drop\n     - source_labels: [__name__]\n       regex: '.*_total'\n       action: keep  # Only keep counters\n   ```\n\n6. **Restart with New Configuration**\n   ```bash\n   # Edit prometheus.yml with changes from steps 3-5\n\n   # Validate config\n   promtool check config /etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml\n\n   # Restart\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n\n   # Monitor startup\n   journalctl -u prometheus -f\n\n   # Wait for compaction to stabilize\n   sleep 300\n   ```\n\n7. **Monitor Memory Usage During Compaction**\n   ```bash\n   # Watch memory spike during next compaction window\n   # (typically 2-4 hours after restart)\n   watch -n 1 'ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep | awk \"{print \\$6/1024 \\\" MB\\\"}\"'\n\n   # Should not exceed allocated memory\n   # If still hitting limit, further reduce retention/cardinality\n   ```\n\n**Prevention:**\n```bash\n# Set memory requests and limits based on cardinality\n# Low cardinality (< 100k series): 8 GB\n# Medium cardinality (100k - 1M): 16-32 GB\n# High cardinality (> 1M): 64+ GB\n\n# Monitor memory usage trend\ncurl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep 'go_memstats_heap_alloc_bytes'\n\n# Set up memory usage alerting\n- alert: PrometheusOOMRisk\n  expr: go_memstats_heap_alloc_bytes / go_memstats_heap_limit_bytes > 0.8\n  for: 5m\n  annotations:\n    summary: \"Prometheus memory usage at {{ $value | humanizePercentage }}\"\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. scrape_interval: 15s\n  evaluation_interval: 15s\n  external_labels:\n    cluster: 'prod'\n\nstorage:\n  tsdb:\n    # Block duration: balance between query latency and compaction memory\n    min_block_duration: 2h    # Creates blocks this often\n    max_block_duration: 2h    # Max size before forcing compaction\n\n    # Retention: based on available disk and query SLA\n    retention:\n      time: 15d                # Keep 15 days of data\n      size: '100GB'            # OR cap at 100GB, whichever comes first\n\n    # WAL settings: balance between durability and performance\n    wal:\n      compression: snappy      # Reduce WAL disk usage\n      segment_size: 128m       # Default is fine\n\n    # Sample density: more samples per chunk = better compression\n    samples_per_chunk: 4096    # Increase from default 1024\n\n    # Out-of-order support (memory cost)\n    out_of_order_time_window: 1h  # Or disable (0) if not needed\n\n    # Chunk segment size: larger = fewer I/O but more memory\n    max_block_chunk_segment_size: 33554432  # 32MB default\n```\n\n---\n\n## Quick Reference\n\n| Issue | Command | Expected Result |\n|-------|---------|-----------------|\n| Check
